      SELECT DISTINCT `t0`.`tag_name`

          INNER JOIN `Tags` AS `t` ON `p0`.`tag_id` = `t`.`tag_id`
          WHERE `p`.`post_id` = `p0`.`post_id`)), 0) AS `Count`
      FROM `Posts` AS `p`
      GROUP BY `p`.`user_id`

      SELECT `p`.`user_id` AS `Id`, COALESCE(SUM((
